the Company has duly caused this report to be signed on its behalf by the
undersigned hereunto duly authorized.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Peregrine
Systems<sup>&#174;</sup> Announces Financial Results for</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fiscal
2004 First Quarter Ended June 30, 2003</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SAN DIEGO, Sept. 9, 2004</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> &#151; Peregrine Systems, Inc. (OTC: PRGN), a
leading provider of asset and service management solutions, today released
historical financial results for the fiscal 2004 first quarter ended June 30,
2003.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The filing of Peregrine&#146;s
fiscal 2004 first quarter 10-Q was delayed due to Peregrine&#146;s prior financial
restatement, voluntary Chapter 11 bankruptcy reorganization proceedings and
restructuring activities.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As a result of Peregrine&#146;s
emergence from reorganization proceedings on Aug. 7, 2003, the company intends
to adopt fresh-start reporting in the fiscal year 2004 second quarter
ended Sept. 30, 2003 in accordance with GAAP (Generally Accepted Accounting
Principles).</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Historical GAAP Financial Results
and Highlights:</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in -19.9pt .0001pt 0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>
  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.4%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="96%" colspan="2" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:96.6%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total revenues for the fiscal 2004 first quarter
  were $42.5 million, a decrease of 14 percent over the same period of the
  preceding year. The fiscal 2003 first quarter total revenues were $49.5
  million, which included approximately $6.7 million from non-core products
  that were subsequently divested during fiscal 2003. The company&#146;s core
  products consist primarily of AssetCenter<sup>&#174; </sup>and ServiceCenter<sup>&#174;</sup>.</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.4%;">

  </td>
  <td width="96%" colspan="2" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:96.6%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.4%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.34%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="93%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:93.26%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Total license revenues for the fiscal 2004 first
  quarter were $12.5 million, a decline of approximately 4 percent when
  compared with the fiscal 2003 first quarter license revenue of $13.0 million.
  Of the total core license revenue in the fiscal 2004 first quarter,
  approximately $7.5 million was for license transactions initiated in the
  quarter, while approximately $5.0 million was attributable to transactions
  initiated prior to fiscal 2003. The $5.0 million in revenue was included as
  part of the fiscal 2004 first quarter revenue because the revenue recognition
  criteria for these transactions were not met until this period.</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.4%;">

  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.34%;">

  </td>
  <td width="93%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:93.26%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.4%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.34%;">

  </td>

  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The fiscal 2003 first quarter license revenue
  included approximately $1.0 million in revenues for non-core products. Of the
  total core license revenue in the fiscal 2003 first quarter, approximately
  $2.2 million was for license transactions initiated in the quarter, while
  approximately $9.7 million was attributable to transactions initiated prior
  to fiscal 2003.</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.4%;">

  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net loss totaled $9.1 million, or $0.05 per share,
  on 196 million diluted shares outstanding in the fiscal 2004 first quarter,
  compared with a net loss of $79.6 million, or $0.40 per share, on 195 million
  diluted shares outstanding for the same period of the preceding year. In the
  fiscal 2004 first quarter, income from continuing operations before
  reorganization items, interest and income taxes was $1.3 million.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Historical Non-GAAP Pro
Forma Financial Results:</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>
  <td width="3%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.3%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="96%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:96.7%;">
  <p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Peregrine reported a non-GAAP pro forma net loss of
  $3.0 million in the fiscal 2004 first quarter, or $0.02 per diluted share,
  compared with a non-GAAP pro forma net loss of $71.0 million, or $0.36 per
  diluted share, in the fiscal 2003 first quarter. The non-GAAP pro forma
  results exclude bankruptcy reorganization, restructuring and impairments.</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The company has reconciled the non-GAAP pro forma net loss to GAAP net
loss in the table below (in thousands, except diluted EPS).&#160; The pro forma net loss is not prepared in
accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States,
and may be different from non-GAAP financial measures used by other
companies.&#160; Non-GAAP financial measures
should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to, measures of
financial performance prepared in accordance to GAAP.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Peregrine uses non-GAAP pro forma information in analyzing financial
results because Peregrine management believes that it provides meaningful
information regarding the company&#146;s operating performance and facilitates
management&#146;s internal comparisons to the company&#146;s historical and current
operating results and to the operating results of other companies.&#160; The company believes that non-GAAP pro forma information
is useful to investors because it allows for greater transparency of the
company&#146;s operating performance.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Management Commentary</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Our financial results for the first quarter of fiscal 2004 provide
clear evidence of a positive trend in Peregrine&#146;s return to operational
stability,&#148; said John Mutch, Peregrine&#146;s president and CEO.&#160; &#147;We were able to dramatically reduce our
operating costs during the first quarter, while slightly increasing our license
and maintenance revenue from our core products over the same period of the
preceding year.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Fresh-Start Reporting</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fresh-start reporting requires that the company adjust the
historical cost of its assets and liabilities to their fair value, effective
July 18, 2003, the date of approval of the company&#146;s plan of
reorganization.&#160; Accordingly, the company
will re-value its balance sheet in the fiscal 2004 second quarter, which
includes adjusting the value of current assets, property and equipment,
intangible assets, accrued liabilities, deferred revenue and stockholders&#146;
equity for the effects of the company&#146;s plan of reorganization.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The fair value of the new common stock for the reorganized company was
determined by management to be $270 million, which represents the company&#146;s
enterprise value adjusted for debt financing, net of cash.&#160; The non-trade debt of the reorganized company
totals approximately $86 million as of August 2003, including secured factor
loans, senior notes and non-interest bearing notes issued to satisfy
pre-petition debt.&#160; As a result of
fresh-start reporting, it may be difficult to compare financial results for the
fiscal 2004 second quarter with other quarters of fiscal year 2004 as well as the
quarters in prior fiscal years.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Conference Call</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Management has scheduled a conference call to discuss its historical
fiscal 2004 first quarter results on Thursday, Sept. 9, at 2:00 p.m. PDT (5:00
p.m. EDT).&#160; Participants should call
(800) 289-0746 or (913) 981-5573 and reference confirmation code 947629.&#160; A replay of the call will be available
beginning Sept. 9 until Sept. 16 by dialing (888) 203-1112 or (719) 457-0820
and entering confirmation code 947629.&#160;
Additionally, a transcript of the conference call will be archived on
the company&#146;s Web site through Sept. 16.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">About Peregrine Systems</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Peregrine Systems, Inc. develops enterprise software solutions that
enable organizations to evolve their IT service and asset management practices
for reduced costs, improved IT productivity and service, and lower risk.&#160; The company&#146;s asset and service management
offerings &#151; such as Service Control and Expense Control - address specific
business problems.&#160; These solutions make
it possible for IT organizations to maintain a changing IT infrastructure,
manage their relationships with end-users and service providers, and gain
greater visibility into the how IT investments are performing.&#160; The Peregrine Evolution Model provides a
roadmap for companies that want to systematically evolve the sophistication and
effectiveness of their IT operating practices.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Founded in 1981, Peregrine Systems has sustained a rich tradition of
delivering solutions with superior functionality to a broad segment of the
global enterprise customer market.&#160;
Headquartered in San Diego, Calif., the company conducts business from
offices in the Americas, Europe, and Asia Pacific.</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"># # #</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

and ServiceCenter are registered trademarks of Peregrine Systems, Inc. or its affiliates.
All other marks are the property of their respective owners.</font></i></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Risk Factors</font></b></p>

<p style="color:windowtext;margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The financial results described in this press release
are historical, in part because the company has significant deficiencies,
including material weaknesses, in its internal controls over financial
reporting.&#160; Until the company&#146;s periodic
reports are current, investors will not have current financial
information.&#160; For this reason and based
on the other risk factors described in the company&#146;s Form 10-K for the fiscal
year ended March 31, 2003 filed April 30, 2004, the company believes trading in
its securities at this time is highly speculative and involves a high degree of
risk.</font></p>
